               <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary mt-1">

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bhs9a5otro5d/src/components/resume/ResumeUploader.tsx]
Thought: 
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
import React, { useCallback, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { Upload, FileText, X, CheckCircle2, AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

// 支持的文件格式
const ACCEPTED_TYPES: Record<string, string> = {
  'application/pdf': 'PDF',
  'application/msword': 'DOC',
  'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document': 'DOCX',
  'text/csv': 'CSV',
  'application/vnd.ms-excel': 'XLS',
  'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet': 'XLSX',
  'text/plain': 'TXT',
};
const ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS = ['.pdf', '.doc', '.docx', '.csv', '.xls', '.xlsx', '.txt'];
const MAX_SIZE_MB = 10;
const MAX_SIZE_BYTES = MAX_SIZE_MB * 1024 * 1024;

interface UploadState {
  status: 'idle' | 'uploading' | 'success' | 'error';
  progress: number;
  fileName: string;
  errorMsg: string;
}

interface ResumeUploaderProps {
  resumeId: string;
  onUploadComplete: (fileUrl: string, fileName: string, fileSize: number, fileType: string) => void;
}

export function ResumeUploader({ resumeId, onUploadComplete }: ResumeUploaderProps) {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [uploadState, setUploadState] = useState<UploadState>({
    status: 'idle', progress: 0, fileName: '', errorMsg: '',
  });

  const validateFile = (file: File): string | null => {
    const mimeOk = Object.keys(ACCEPTED_TYPES).includes(file.type);
    const extOk = ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS.some(ext =>
      file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith(ext)
    );
    if (!mimeOk && !extOk) {
      return `不支持该文件格式，请上传 ${ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS.join(' / ')} 格式的文件`;
    }
    if (file.size > MAX_SIZE_BYTES) {
      return `文件大小不能超过 ${MAX_SIZE_MB}MB（当前 ${(file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1)}MB）`;
    }
    return null;
  };

  const uploadFile = useCallback(async (file: File) => {
    if (!user) return;

    const validationError = validateFile(file);
    if (validationError) {
      setUploadState({ status: 'error', progress: 0, fileName: file.name, errorMsg: validationError });
      return;
    }

    setUploadState({ status: 'uploading', progress: 5, fileName: file.name, errorMsg: '' });

    // 构造文件路径：user_id/resume_id/filename（保证唯一性）
    const ext = file.name.substring(file.name.lastIndexOf('.'));
    const safeName = file.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._\u4e00-\u9fa5-]/g, '_');
    const filePath = `${user.id}/${resumeId}/${Date.now()}_${safeName}`;

    // 模拟进度 - Supabase 客户端上传不暴露进度回调，用定时器模拟
    let fakeProgress = 5;
    const progressTimer = setInterval(() => {
      fakeProgress = Math.min(fakeProgress + Math.random() * 15, 85);
      setUploadState(prev => ({ ...prev, progress: Math.round(fakeProgress) }));
    }, 200);

    const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
      .from('resumes')
      .upload(filePath, file, {
        cacheControl: '3600',
        upsert: false,
        contentType: file.type || 'application/octet-stream',
      });

    clearInterval(progressTimer);

    if (uploadError) {
      setUploadState({
        status: 'error', progress: 0, fileName: file.name,
        errorMsg: uploadError.message || '文件上传失败，请重试',
      });
      toast.error('文件上传失败');
      return;
    }

    // 获取私有文件的签名 URL（有效期1年）
    const { data: urlData, error: urlError } = await supabase.storage
      .from('resumes')
      .createSignedUrl(filePath, 60 * 60 * 24 * 365);

    if (urlError || !urlData) {
      setUploadState({
        status: 'error', progress: 0, fileName: file.name,
        errorMsg: '获取文件链接失败',
      });
      return;
    }

    setUploadState({ status: 'success', progress: 100, fileName: file.name, errorMsg: '' });
    toast.success('文件上传成功');

    const fileType = ACCEPTED_TYPES[file.type] || ext.replace('.', '').toUpperCase();
    onUploadComplete(urlData.signedUrl, file.name, file.size, fileType);
  }, [user, resumeId, onUploadComplete]);

  // 拖拽处理
  const handleDragOver = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(true);
  };
  const handleDragLeave = () => setIsDragging(false);
  const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(false);
    const file = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
    if (file) uploadFile(file);
  };
  const handleFileChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (file) uploadFile(file);
    // 清空 input 以允许重复选同一文件
    e.target.value = '';
  };

  const handleReset = () => {
    setUploadState({ status: 'idle', progress: 0, fileName: '', errorMsg: '' });
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-3">
      {/* 拖拽区域 */}
      {uploadState.status === 'idle' && (
        <div
          onDragOver={handleDragOver}
          onDragLeave={handleDragLeave}
          onDrop={handleDrop}
          onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}
          className={cn(
            'relative border-2 border-dashed rounded-lg p-6 text-center cursor-pointer transition-colors select-none',
            isDragging
              ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5'
              : 'border-border hover:border-primary/50 hover:bg-muted/30'
          )}
        >
          <Upload className={cn(
            'w-8 h-8 mx-auto mb-3 transition-colors',
            isDragging ? 'text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground'
          )} />
          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
            {isDragging ? '松开鼠标上传文件' : '拖拽文件至此，或点击选择文件'}
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1.5">
            支持 PDF · Word（DOC/DOCX）· CSV · Excel · TXT，最大 {MAX_SIZE_MB}MB
          </p>
          <input
            ref={inputRef}
            type="file"
            accept={ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS.join(',')}
            className="hidden"
            onChange={handleFileChange}
          />
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 上传中 */}
      {uploadState.status === 'uploading' && (
        <div className="border border-border rounded-lg p-4 space-y-3">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
            <FileText className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
            <span className="text-sm text-foreground truncate flex-1 min-w-0">
              {uploadState.fileName}
            </span>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">{uploadState.progress}%</span>
          </div>
          <Progress value={uploadState.progress} className="h-1.5" />
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">正在上传，请稍候…</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 上传成功 */}
      {uploadState.status === 'success' && (
        <div className="border border-primary/30 bg-primary/5 rounded-lg p-4 flex items-center gap-3">
          <CheckCircle2 className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate">{uploadState.fileName}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">上传成功</p>
          </div>
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            className="h-7 w-7 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
            onClick={handleReset}
            title="重新上传"
          >
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 上传失败 */}
      {uploadState.status === 'error' && (
        <div className="border border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/5 rounded-lg p-4 space-y-2">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
            <AlertCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-destructive shrink-0" />
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate flex-1 min-w-0">
              {uploadState.fileName || '文件上传失败'}
            </p>
          </div>
          <p className="text-xs text-destructive pl-8">{uploadState.errorMsg}</p>
          <div className="pl-8">
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="h-7 text-xs" onClick={handleReset}>
              重新选择
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// 文件格式图标颜色映射
const FILE_TYPE_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
  PDF: 'text-destructive',
  DOC: 'text-primary',
  DOCX: 'text-primary',
  CSV: 'text-chart-2',
  XLS: 'text-chart-2',
  XLSX: 'text-chart-2',
  TXT: 'text-muted-foreground',
};

function formatFileSize(bytes?: number): string {
  if (!bytes) return '未知大小';
  if (bytes < 1024) return `${bytes} B`;
  if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return `${(bytes / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB`;
  return `${(bytes / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1)} MB`;
}

```
New String: ```
export default function ResumeManagement() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [resumes, setResumes] = useState<Resume[]>([]);
  const [capability, setCapability] = useState<CapabilityData | null>(null);
  const [templates, setTemplates] = useState<IndustryTemplate[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [radarData, setRadarData] = useState(DEFAULT_RADAR_DATA);
  const [addDialogOpen, setAddDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [newResumeTitle, setNewResumeTitle] = useState('');
  const [selectedIndustry, setSelectedIndustry] = useState('tech');
  // 当前正在上传文件的简历 ID
  const [uploadingResumeId, setUploadingResumeId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (user) {
      fetchResumes();
      fetchCapabilityData();
      fetchTemplates();
    }
  }, [user]);

  const fetchResumes = async () => {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('resumes')
      .select('*')
      .eq('profile_id', user!.id)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false });
    setResumes(Array.isArray(data) ? data as Resume[] : []);
    setLoading(false);
  };

  const fetchCapabilityData = async () => {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('capability_data')
      .select('*')
      .eq('profile_id', user!.id)
      .maybeSingle();
    if (data) {
      setCapability(data as CapabilityData);
      const rd = data.radar_data as Record<string, number>;
      if (rd && Object.keys(rd).length > 0) {
        setRadarData(Object.entries(rd).map(([subject, value]) => ({ subject, value })));
      }
    }
  };

  const fetchTemplates = async () => {
    const { data } = await supabase.from('industry_templates').select('*').order('label');
    setTemplates(Array.isArray(data) ? data as IndustryTemplate[] : []);
  };

  const handleAddResume = async () => {
    if (!newResumeTitle.trim()) return;
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('resumes')
      .insert({
        profile_id: user!.id,
        title: newResumeTitle,
        is_primary: resumes.length === 0,
      })
      .select()
      .maybeSingle();
    if (error) { toast.error('创建简历失败'); return; }
    toast.success('简历已创建，可立即上传文件');
    setAddDialogOpen(false);
    setNewResumeTitle('');
    // 创建后自动展开上传区
    if (data?.id) setUploadingResumeId(data.id);
    fetchResumes();
  };

  const handleDeleteResume = async (resume: Resume) => {
    // 若有附件先从 Storage 删除
    if (resume.file_url && resume.file_name) {
      const filePath = `${user!.id}/${resume.id}`;
      await supabase.storage.from('resumes').remove([filePath]);
    }
    const { error } = await supabase.from('resumes').delete().eq('id', resume.id);
    if (error) { toast.error('删除失败'); return; }
    toast.success('简历已删除');
    if (uploadingResumeId === resume.id) setUploadingResumeId(null);
    fetchResumes();
  };

  const handleSetPrimary = async (id: string) => {
    await supabase.from('resumes').update({ is_primary: false }).eq('profile_id', user!.id);
    await supabase.from('resumes').update({ is_primary: true }).eq('id', id);
    fetchResumes();
    toast.success('已设为主简历');
  };

  // 上传完成回调 —— 更新数据库中的文件字段
  const handleUploadComplete = async (
    resumeId: string,
    fileUrl: string,
    fileName: string,
    fileSize: number,
    fileType: string,
  ) => {
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from('resumes')
      .update({
        file_url: fileUrl,
        file_name: fileName,
        file_size: fileSize,
        file_type: fileType,
        uploaded_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .eq('id', resumeId);
    if (error) { toast.error('文件信息保存失败'); return; }
    setUploadingResumeId(null);
    fetchResumes();
  };

  const handleDownload = async (resume: Resume) => {
    if (!resume.file_url) return;
    try {
      const link = document.createElement('a');
      link.href = resume.file_url;
      link.download = resume.file_name || '简历文件';
      link.target = '_blank';
      link.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
      document.body.appendChild(link);
      link.click();
      document.body.removeChild(link);
    } catch {
      toast.error('下载失败，请重试');
    }
  };

  const handleSaveCapability = async () => {
    const radarObj: Record<string, number> = {};
    radarData.forEach(item => { radarObj[item.subject] = item.value; });

    const currentTemplate = templates.find(t => t.industry === selectedIndustry);
    const treeData = currentTemplate ? currentTemplate.skill_tree : DEFAULT_TREE;

    if (capability) {
      await supabase.from('capability_data')
        .update({ radar_data: radarObj, tree_data: treeData, industry: selectedIndustry })
        .eq('id', capability.id);
    } else {
      await supabase.from('capability_data').insert({
        profile_id: user!.id,
        industry: selectedIndustry,
        radar_data: radarObj,
        tree_data: treeData,
        skills: radarData.map(r => ({ name: r.subject, level: r.value })),
      });
    }
    toast.success('能力数据已保存');
    fetchCapabilityData();
  };

  const currentTemplate = templates.find(t => t.industry === selectedIndustry);
  const treeData = (capability?.tree_data && Object.keys(capability.tree_data).length > 0)
    ? capability.tree_data
    : currentTemplate?.skill_tree || DEFAULT_TREE;

  return (
    <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 md:px-8 py-6 space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground text-balance">简历管理</h1>
        <Dialog open={addDialogOpen} onOpenChange={setAddDialogOpen}>
          <DialogTrigger asChild>
            <Button size="sm">
              <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />新建简历
            </Button>
          </DialogTrigger>
          <DialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
            <DialogHeader>
              <DialogTitle>新建简历</DialogTitle>
            </DialogHeader>
            <div className="space-y-4 pt-2">
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <Label className="text-sm font-normal">简历名称</Label>
                <Input
                  placeholder="例如：前端开发岗位简历"
                  value={newResumeTitle}
                  onChange={e => setNewResumeTitle(e.target.value)}
                  onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleAddResume()}
                  className="px-3"
                />
              </div>
              <Button onClick={handleAddResume} className="w-full h-9">创建并上传文件</Button>
            </div>
          </DialogContent>
        </Dialog>
      </div>

      {/* 简历列表 */}
      <Card>
        <CardHeader className="pb-3">
          <CardTitle className="text-base flex items-center gap-2">
            <FileText className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
            我的简历
          </CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          {loading ? (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {Array(3).fill(0).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-16 bg-muted" />)}
            </div>
          ) : resumes.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="py-10 text-center">
              <Upload className="w-10 h-10 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-3" />
              <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">暂无简历，点击"新建简历"开始上传</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {resumes.map(resume => (
                <div key={resume.id} className="rounded-md border border-border overflow-hidden">
                  {/* 简历行 */}
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 hover:bg-muted/30 transition-colors">
                    {/* 文件格式图标 */}
                    <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-md bg-muted flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                      {resume.file_type ? (
                        <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold ${FILE_TYPE_COLOR[resume.file_type] ?? 'text-muted-foreground'}`}>
                          {resume.file_type}
                        </span>
                      ) : (
                        <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* 信息区 */}
                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                        <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate text-sm">{resume.title}</span>
                        {resume.is_primary && (
                          <Badge className="text-xs bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/20">主简历</Badge>
                        )}
                        {resume.file_type && (
                          <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs">{resume.file_type}</Badge>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-0.5 flex-wrap">
                        {resume.file_name ? (
                          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate max-w-[200px]">
                            {resume.file_name}
                          </span>
                        ) : (
                          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground italic">未上传文件</span>
                        )}
                        {resume.file_size && (
                          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                            {formatFileSize(resume.file_size)}
                          </span>
                        )}
                        <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                          {new Date(resume.updated_at).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN')}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* 操作区 */}
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
                      {/* 上传/替换文件 */}
                      <Button
                        variant="ghost"
                        size="icon"
                        className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground hover:text-primary"
                        title={resume.file_url ? '替换文件' : '上传文件'}
                        onClick={() => setUploadingResumeId(
                          uploadingResumeId === resume.id ? null : resume.id
                        )}
                      >
                        <Upload className="w-4 h-4" />
                      </Button>
                      {/* 下载 */}
                      {resume.file_url && (
                        <Button
                          variant="ghost"
                          size="icon"
                          className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground hover:text-primary"
                          title="下载文件"
                          onClick={() => handleDownload(resume)}
                        >
                          <Download className="w-4 h-4" />
                        </Button>
                      )}
                      {/* 设为主简历 */}
                      {!resume.is_primary && (
                        <Button
                          variant="ghost"
                          size="icon"
                          className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
                          title="设为主简历"
                          onClick={() => handleSetPrimary(resume.id)}
                        >
                          <Star className="w-4 h-4" />
                        </Button>
                      )}
                      {/* 删除 */}
                      <AlertDialog>
                        <AlertDialogTrigger asChild>
                          <Button
                            variant="ghost"
                            size="icon"
                            className="h-8 w-8 text-destructive hover:text-destructive"
                          >
                            <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
                          </Button>
                        </AlertDialogTrigger>
                        <AlertDialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
                          <AlertDialogHeader>
                            <AlertDialogTitle>确认删除简历</AlertDialogTitle>
                            <AlertDialogDescription>
                              将同时删除简历记录及已上传的文件（如有），此操作不可恢复。
                            </AlertDialogDescription>
                          </AlertDialogHeader>
                          <AlertDialogFooter>
                            <AlertDialogCancel>取消</AlertDialogCancel>
                            <AlertDialogAction
                              className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/90"
                              onClick={() => handleDeleteResume(resume)}
                            >
                              确认删除
                            </AlertDialogAction>
                          </AlertDialogFooter>
                        </AlertDialogContent>
                      </AlertDialog>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* 展开的上传区域 */}
                  {uploadingResumeId === resume.id && (
                    <div className="border-t border-border bg-muted/20 p-4">
                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-3">
                        {resume.file_url ? '替换已有文件（原文件将被覆盖）' : '上传简历文件'}
                      </p>
                      <ResumeUploader
                        resumeId={resume.id}
                        onUploadComplete={(url, name, size, type) =>
                          handleUploadComplete(resume.id, url, name, size, type)
                        }
                      />
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* 文件格式说明 */}
      <Card className="bg-muted/30 border-dashed">
        <CardContent className="p-4">
          <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
            <FileType className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
            <div>
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">支持的文件格式</p>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2">
                {[
                  { type: 'PDF', color: 'text-destructive' },
                  { type: 'DOCX', color: 'text-primary' },
                  { type: 'DOC', color: 'text-primary' },
                  { type: 'CSV', color: 'text-chart-2' },
                  { type: 'XLSX', color: 'text-chart-2' },
                  { type: 'XLS', color: 'text-chart-2' },
                  { type: 'TXT', color: 'text-muted-foreground' },
                ].map(({ type, color }) => (
                  <Badge key={type} variant="secondary" className={`text-xs font-mono ${color}`}>
                    {type}
                  </Badge>
                ))}
              </div>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-2">单个文件最大 10MB</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* 能力图谱 */}
      <Card>
        <CardHeader className="pb-3">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 flex-wrap">
            <CardTitle className="text-base">能力图谱</CardTitle>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <select
                value={selectedIndustry}
                onChange={e => setSelectedIndustry(e.target.value)}
                className="text-sm border border-border rounded-md px-2 py-1 bg-background text-foreground"
              >
                {templates.map(t => (
                  <option key={t.industry} value={t.industry}>{t.label}</option>
                ))}
              </select>
              <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={handleSaveCapability}>
                <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-1.5" />保存
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <Tabs defaultValue="radar">
            <TabsList className="mb-4">
              <TabsTrigger value="radar">雷达图</TabsTrigger>
              <TabsTrigger value="tree">能力树</TabsTrigger>
              <TabsTrigger value="simulate">能力模拟</TabsTrigger>
            </TabsList>

            <TabsContent value="radar">
              <CapabilityRadarChart data={radarData} height={300} />
            </TabsContent>

            <TabsContent value="tree">
              <CapabilityTreeChart data={treeData} />
            </TabsContent>

            <TabsContent value="simulate">
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4 text-pretty">
                拖动滑块模拟能力值变化，查看对岗位匹配度的影响
              </p>
              <div className="space-y-5">
                {radarData.map((item, idx) => (
                  <div key={item.subject} className="space-y-2">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                      <Label className="text-sm font-normal">{item.subject}</Label>
                      <span className="text-sm font-medium text-primary w-8 text-right">{item.value}</span>
                    </div>
                    <Slider
                      value={[item.value]}
                      onValueChange={([v]) => {
                        const updated = [...radarData];
                        updated[idx] = { ...item, value: v };
                        setRadarData(updated);
                      }}
                      min={0}
                      max={100}
                      step={5}
                      className="w-full"
                    />
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
              <div className="mt-6 p-4 bg-primary/5 rounded-md border border-primary/20">
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-primary">综合匹配度预测</p>
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary mt-1">
                  {Math.round(radarData.reduce((s, i) => s + i.value, 0) / radarData.length)}%
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">基于当前能力值估算</p>
              </div>
            </TabsContent>
          </Tabs>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}
```

应用描述\n本系统是一款基于AI智能体技术的双向招聘匹配平台,为求职者和企业提供智能化的岗位匹配服务。系统通过AI对话、能力图谱可视化、智能简历解析等功能,实现求职者与企业岗位的精准匹配,提升招聘效率。\n\n## 2. 用户与使用场景\n\n### 2.1 目标用户\n- 求职者:需要快速找到匹配岗位的求职人员\n- 企业HR:需要高效筛选候选人的招聘人员\n- 平台管理员:负责系统运营与维护的管理人员\n\n### 2.2 核心使用场景\n- 求职者通过AI对话快速匹配适合岗位\n- 企业发布职位并获得智能推荐的候选人\n- 双方通过能力图谱直观了解匹配度\n- 管理员监控平台运营数据并进行用户管理\n\n## 3. 页面结构与功能说明\n\n### 3.1 整体结构\n```\n├── 求职者端(移动端)\n│   ├── 首页\n│   ├── 简历管理\n│   ├── 职位详情与申请\n│   ├── AI匹配与对话\n│   └── 个人中心\n├── 企业端(移动端)\n│   ├── 首页\n│   ├── 人才库管理\n│   ├── 招聘流程管理\n│   ├── 双向沟通\n│   └── 数据统计\n└── 管理后台(Web端)\n    ├── 用户管理\n    ├── 数据维护\n    └── 运营监控\n```\n\n### 3.2 求职者端功能\n\n#### 3.2.1 首页\n- 个性化职位推荐:基于用户历史行为、浏览记录及偏好设置,展示推荐职位列表\n- 快速搜索与筛选:支持关键词搜索,按地区、薪资、行业等条件筛选职位\n\n#### 3.2.2 简历管理\n- 简历文件上传:支持Word(.doc/.docx)、PDF(.pdf)、CSV(.csv)等格式简历文件上传,提供拖拽上传和点击上传两种方式,显示文件上传进度\n- 简历文件存储:上传的简历文件存储在Supabase Storage中\n- 已上传简历列表:展示已上传简历文件列表,包含文件名、格式、大小、上传时间等信息\n- 简历文件管理:支持下载、删除已上传的简历文件\n- 简历预览:在线查看已上传简历内容\n- 简历编辑:支持在线修改简历信息\n- 能力发展中心:展示个人能力雷达图和能力树图,可视化呈现技能掌握情况\n- 能力模拟:支持拖拽方式模拟能力值变化,查看对匹配度的影响\n\n#### 3.2.3 职位详情与申请\n- 职位详情展示:显示职位描述、任职要求、公司简介、工作环境等完整信息\n- 智能匹配度分析:展示个人简历与职位要求的匹配度评分及详细分析\n- 一键申请:快速提交职位申请\n- 职位收藏:收藏感兴趣的职位便于后续查看\n\n#### 3.2.4 AI匹配与对话\n- AI智能对话:通过语音或文字与AI助手进行多轮对话,描述求职意向\n- 匹配报告展示:查看AI对话记录及生成的匹配报告,包括匹配亮点、待改进点及建议\n- 批注与反馈:对匹配结果进行批注和反馈\n\n#### 3.2.5 个人中心\n- 个人信息管理:查看和修改基本信息、教育背景、工作经历等\n- 发展报告查看:查看个人发展报告与匹配分析报告\n- 系统设置:调整界面风格、通知方式等个性化设置\n- 用户反馈:提交意见和建议\n\n### 3.3 企业端功能\n\n#### 3.3.1 首页\n- 个性化人才推荐:基于发布的职位需求,展示高匹配度候选人列表\n- 快速职位发布:通过语音或文字输入职位需求,系统自动生成职位描述\n- 职位管理:查看、编辑、删除已发布职位\n\n#### 3.3.2 人才库管理\n- 智能人才筛选:按技能标签、项目经验、教育背景等条件筛选候选人\n- 人才搜索:支持关键词搜索候选人\n- 能力图谱对比:查看候选人能力图谱与岗位需求的匹配热力图\n- 多候选人对比:同时对比多个候选人的能力图谱\n\n#### 3.3.3 招聘流程管理\n- AI面试:发起AI模拟面试,系统自动生成结构化问题\n- 面试评估:查看AI生成的多维评估报告,包括沟通能力、专业水平、岗位适配度等\n- 候选人标记:标记候选人状态(感兴趣/待定/不匹配)\n- 招聘看板:查看候选人在招聘流程中的状态(初筛/面试/录用)\n\n#### 3.3.4 双向沟通\n- 智能对话:与候选人进行实时沟通,系统提供标准化回复模板\n- 语音转文字:支持语音输入自动转换为文字\n- 任务分配:团队成员间分配招聘任务\n\n#### 3.3.5 数据统计\n- 招聘数据看板:展示渠道来源、面试通过率、录用周期等关键指标\n- 行业趋势洞察:查看行业人才流动报告,包括热门技能、薪资水平等\n\n### 3.4 管理后台功能\n\n#### 3.4.1 用户管理\n- 用户信息查看:查看求职者和企业用户的注册信息\n- 用户审核:审核新注册用户\n- 权限设置:设置不同用户的访问权限\n- 用户行为分析:分析用户使用行为数据\n\n#### 3.4.2 数据维护\n- 数据异常监测:实时监测系统数据异常情况\n- 数据备份:定期备份系统数据\n- 数据恢复:在数据丢失时进行恢复操作\n\n#### 3.4.3 运营监控\n- 平台运行数据收集:实时收集平台各项运行数据\n- 可视化报表:生成平台运营数据的可视化报表\n- 异常预警:当平台出现异常时及时预警\n\n## 4. 业务规则与逻辑\n\n### 4.1 核心匹配机制\n\n#### 4.1.1 匹配计算规则\n- 采用双引擎模式:结构化匹配(70%)+ 规则匹配(30%)\n- 结构化匹配:基于六大行业能力树模板(互联网/科技、金融/投资等),对齐简历与岗位结构,通过节点权重计算匹配度\n- 规则匹配:提取城市、薪资等信息进行量化评分\n- 学历惩罚机制:企业可自定义学历不匹配的惩罚系数(0-100%)\n- 最终匹配度 = 结构化匹配得分 × 70% + 规则匹配得分 × 30% - 学历惩罚\n\n#### 4.1.2 行业识别与模板加载\n- 系统自动识别简历和职位所属行业\n- 根据行业类型加载对应的能力树模板\n- 支持六大行业:互联网/科技、金融/投资、制造业、教育培训、医疗健康、其他\n\n#### 4.1.3 匹配报告生成\n- 生成包含匹配度评分、优势分析、差距建议的详细报告\n- 双向展示:求职者端显示适合岗位,企业端显示推荐候选人\n\n### 4.2 AI对话匹配流程\n- 用户发起对话,描述需求(求职意向或岗位要求)\n- AI助手进行多轮对话,深入理解需求细节\n- 系统基于对话内容进行智能解析和结构化数据提取\n- 执行匹配计算,生成匹配结果\n- 向用户展示匹配报告并提供优化建议\n\n### 4.3 动态反馈优化机制\n- 收集用户行为数据(浏览、申请、收藏等)\n- 收集用户反馈(满意度评价、批注等)\n- 基于数据分析动态调整推荐算法权重\n- 持续优化匹配精准度\n\n### 4.4 简历智能解析规则\n- 自动识别简历中的关键信息:基本信息、教育背景、工作经历、项目经验、技能标签等\n- 提取技能关键词并进行标准化处理\n- 根据目标职位提供简历优化建议\n\n## 5. 异常与边界情况\n\n| 场景 | 异常情况 | 处理方式 |\n|------|----------|----------|\n| 简历上传 | 文件格式不支持 | 提示用户仅支持Word(.doc/.docx)、PDF(.pdf)、CSV(.csv)等格式 |\n| 简历上传 | 文件解析失败 | 提示用户检查文件内容或重新上传 |\n| 简历上传 | 文件上传失败 | 提示用户检查网络连接并支持重试 |\n| AI对话 | 用户输入无法理解 | 引导用户重新描述或提供示例 |\n| 匹配计算 | 简历信息不完整 | 提示用户补充必要信息 |\n| 匹配计算 | 无匹配结果 | 提示用户调整筛选条件或扩大搜索范围 |\n| 职位申请 | 重复申请同一职位 | 提示用户已申请过该职位 |\n| 数据加载 | 网络连接失败 | 提示用户检查网络连接并支持重试 |\n| 用户登录 | 账号密码错误 | 提示错误信息并限制连续错误次数 |\n| 权限访问 | 无权限访问某功能 | 提示权限不足并引导联系管理员 |\n\n## 6. 验收标准\n\n1. 求职者可成功上传简历并查看能力图谱可视化展示\n2. 求职者可通过AI对话获得职位推荐,匹配度计算准确\n3. 求职者可查看职位详情、申请职位、收藏职位\n4. 企业可发布职位并获得候选人推荐\n5. 企业可查看候选人能力图谱并进行对比分析\n6. 企业可发起AI面试并查看评估报告\n7. 双方可通过系统进行实时沟通\n8. 管理员可进行用户管理、数据维护和运营监控\n9. 匹配算法基于用户反馈实现动态优化\n10. 系统在vivo手机环境下运行流畅,界面适配良好\n11. 所有用户数据传输和存储均经过加密处理\n12. 系统响应时间符合性能要求,关键操作在3秒内完成\n\n## 7. 本期不实现功能\n\n1. 多语言翻译功能\n2. 视频面试功能\n3. 第三方招聘平台数据同步\n4. 薪资谈判辅助功能\n5. 职业培训课程推荐\n6. 企业背景调查服务\n7. 候选人背景核查服务\n8. 智能合同生成功能\n9. 入职流程管理功能\n10. 员工绩效跟踪功能'}

运营监控\n```\n\n### 3.2 求职者端功能\n\n#### 3.2.1 首页\n- 个性化职位推荐:基于用户历史行为、浏览记录及偏好设置,展示推荐职位列表\n- 快速搜索与筛选:支持关键词搜索,按地区、薪资、行业等条件筛选职位\n\n#### 3.2.2 简历管理\n- 简历文件上传:支持Word(.doc/.docx)、PDF(.pdf)、CSV(.csv)等格式简历文件上传,提供拖拽上传和点击上传两种方式,显示文件上传进度\n- 简历文件存储:上传的简历文件存储在Supabase Storage中\n- 已上传简历列表:展示已上传简历文件列表,包含文件名、格式、大小、上传时间等信息\n- 简历文件管理:支持下载、删除已上传的简历文件\n- 简历预览:在线查看已上传简历内容\n- 简历编辑:支持在线修改简历信息\n- 能力发展中心:展示个人能力雷达图和能力树图,可视化呈现技能掌握情况\n- 能力模拟:支持拖拽方式模拟能力值变化,查看对匹配度的影响\n\n#### 3.2.3 职位详情与申请\n- 职位详情展示:显示职位描述、任职要求、公司简介、工作环境等完整信息\n- 智能匹配度分析:展示个人简历与职位要求的匹配度评分及详细分析\n- 一键申请:快速提交职位申请\n- 职位收藏:收藏感兴趣的职位便于后续查看\n\n#### 3.2.4 AI匹配与对话\n- AI智能对话:通过语音或文字与AI助手进行多轮对话,描述求职意向\n- 匹配报告展示:查看AI对话记录及生成的匹配报告,包括匹配亮点、待改进点及建议\n- 批注与反馈:对匹配结果进行批注和反馈\n\n#### 3.2.5 个人中心\n- 个人信息管理:查看和修改基本信息、教育背景、工作经历等\n- 发展报告查看:查看个人发展报告与匹配分析报告\n- 系统设置:调整界面风格、通知方式等个性化设置\n- 用户反馈:提交意见和建议\n\n### 3.3 企业端功能\n\n#### 3.3.1 首页\n- 个性化人才推荐:基于发布的职位需求,展示高匹配度候选人列表\n- 快速职位发布:通过语音或文字输入职位需求,系统自动生成职位描述\n- 职位管理:查看、编辑、删除已发布职位\n\n#### 3.3.2 人才库管理\n- 智能人才筛选:按技能标签、项目经验、教育背景等条件筛选候选人\n- 人才搜索:支持关键词搜索候选人\n- 能力图谱对比:查看候选人能力图谱与岗位需求的匹配热力图\n- 多候选人对比:同时对比多个候选人的能力图谱\n\n#### 3.3.3 招聘流程管理\n- AI面试:发起AI模拟面试,系统自动生成结构化问题\n- 面试评估:查看AI生成的多维评估报告,包括沟通能力、专业水平、岗位适配度等\n- 候选人标记:标记候选人状态(感兴趣/待定/不匹配)\n- 招聘看板:查看候选人在招聘流程中的状态(初筛/面试/录用)\n\n#### 3.3.4 双向沟通\n- 智能对话:与候选人进行实时沟通,系统提供标准化回复模板\n- 语音转文字:支持语音输入自动转换为文字\n- 任务分配:团队成员间分配招聘任务\n\n#### 3.3.5 数据统计\n- 招聘数据看板:展示渠道来源、面试通过率、录用周期等关键指标\n- 行业趋势洞察:查看行业人才流动报告,包括热门技能、薪资水平等\n\n### 3.4 管理后台功能\n\n#### 3.4.1 用户管理\n- 用户信息查看:查看求职者和企业用户的注册信息\n- 用户审核:审核新注册用户\n- 权限设置:设置不同用户的访问权限\n- 用户行为分析:分析用户使用行为数据\n\n#### 3.4.2 数据维护\n- 数据异常监测:实时监测系统数据异常情况\n- 数据备份:定期备份系统数据\n- 数据恢复:在数据丢失时进行恢复操作\n\n#### 3.4.3 运营监控\n- 平台运行数据收集:实时收集平台各项运行数据\n- 可视化报表:生成平台运营数据的可视化报表\n- 异常预警:当平台出现异常时及时预警\n\n## 4. 业务规则与逻辑\n\n### 4.1 核心匹配机制\n\n#### 4.1.1 匹配计算规则\n- 采用双引擎模式:结构化匹配(70%)+ 规则匹配(30%)\n- 结构化匹配:基于六大行业能力树模板(互联网/科技、金融/投资等),对齐简历与岗位结构,通过节点权重计算匹配度\n- 规则匹配:提取城市、薪资等信息进行量化评分\n- 学历惩罚机制:企业可自定义学历不匹配的惩罚系数(0-100%)\n- 最终匹配度 = 结构化匹配得分 × 70% + 规则匹配得分 × 30% - 学历惩罚\n\n#### 4.1.2 行业识别与模板加载\n- 系统自动识别简历和职位所属行业\n- 根据行业类型加载对应的能力树模板\n- 支持六大行业:互联网/科技、金融/投资、制造业、教育培训、医疗健康、其他\n\n#### 4.1.3 匹配报告生成\n- 生成包含匹配度评分、优势分析、差距建议的详细报告\n- 双向展示:求职者端显示适合岗位,企业端显示推荐候选人\n\n### 4.2 AI对话匹配流程\n- 用户发起对话,描述需求(求职意向或岗位要求)\n- AI助手进行多轮对话,深入理解需求细节\n- 系统基于对话内容进行智能解析和结构化数据提取\n- 执行匹配计算,生成匹配结果\n- 向用户展示匹配报告并提供优化建议\n\n### 4.3 动态反馈优化机制\n- 收集用户行为数据(浏览、申请、收藏等)\n- 收集用户反馈(满意度评价、批注等)\n- 基于数据分析动态调整推荐算法权重\n- 持续优化匹配精准度\n\n### 4.4 简历智能解析规则\n- 自动识别简历中的关键信息:基本信息、教育背景、工作经历、项目经验、技能标签等\n- 提取技能关键词并进行标准化处理\n- 根据目标职位提供简历优化建议\n\n## 5. 异常与边界情况\n\n| 场景 | <observation>
**MCPObservation**
NAME: aesthetic_template
RESULTS: 基于您提供的《Agent驱动的岗位智能匹配与能力图谱系统》PRD，我为您推导了以下UI/UX设计方案。

**核心视觉风格定义：工具理性与数据可视化风 (Tool Rationality & Data-Driven)**
本系统核心在于“精准匹配”与“能力量化”，设计必须摒弃感性装饰，以极简、克制、高信噪比的界面服务于数据展示与AI交互，传递专业、高效、客观的平台信任感。

---

### 1. Color（配色方案）
- **主背景色**：采用极简冷灰（#F4F5F7）作为全局底色，卡片与内容区使用纯白（#FFFFFF），通过明暗对比构建清晰的信息层级，确保长时间阅读简历不疲劳。
- **主色**：选用沉稳的**深青色（#00796B）**，传递专业、理性的职业感。仅用于核心按钮、AI对话气泡及能力图谱的主视觉线。
- **强调色**：选用**琥珀橙（#FF8F00）**，仅用于匹配度高亮、异常状态提示及核心行动点（如“一键申请”），总彩色数量严格控制在2种。
- **渐变限制**：禁止大面积渐变。仅在AI匹配度得分的环形进度条中，允许使用深青到浅青的同色系微渐变以体现数据流动感。禁止文字与背景同色。

### 2. Layout（布局结构）
- **模块化卡片**：移动端采用全包围式微圆角（4px）卡片承载独立信息块（如职位、简历解析结果），卡片间距固定为16px，拒绝视觉粘连，确保信息独立性。
- **数据可视化优先**：首页与详情页顶部优先展示“能力雷达图”与“匹配度仪表盘”，采用左右分栏或上下结构，确保核心匹配数据第一眼可见。
- **对话式交互区**：AI匹配模块采用底部悬浮输入框+全屏对话流布局，对话气泡采用紧凑型排版，最大化利用屏幕空间展示结构化匹配报告。
- **后台栅格系统**：Web端管理后台采用标准的24栏栅格系统，侧边导航固定，右侧内容区支持自适应缩放，确保海量数据表格的阅读效率。

### 3. Elements（界面元素）
- **图标设计**：全部采用2px线性的几何化图标，无填充、无多余装饰，确保在小尺寸下依然保持极高的辨识度与专业感。禁止使用任何emoji。
- **图谱组件**：能力雷达图与树状图摒弃复杂背景，仅保留极细的网格参考线（#E0E0E0）与半透明的主色数据填充（20%透明度），突出数据本身。
- **表单与输入**：输入框采用下划线或浅灰描边样式，聚焦时边框变为深青色。AI对话框内嵌语音波形可视化组件，波形高度随音量实时变化。
- **标签系统**：技能与行业标签采用浅灰底色（#EBEBEB）加深色文字，摒弃彩色标签，避免界面色彩杂乱，仅通过字号与字重区分主次。

### 4. Motion（动效设计）
- **图谱生长**：进入能力图谱页面时，雷达图多边形或能力树节点采用 `transform: scale` 与 `opacity` 从中心向外呈放射状展开（时长400ms，缓出）。
- **AI对话反馈**：AI生成匹配报告时，采用骨架屏的微弱呼吸效果（`opacity` 0.5至1交替）代替传统的加载圈，降低等待焦虑。
- **数值滚动**：匹配度得分（如从0跳动至85%）采用数字递增动画，配合进度条的 `transform: scaleX` 展开，强化匹配结果的获得感。
- **物理触感**：移动端所有可点击卡片与按钮，在按下时触发轻微的缩放（`scale(0.98)`），模拟真实按压阻尼，提升操作确认感。避免使用复杂动画库。
</observation>

     1 import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2 import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

     6 import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';

    11 import { Eye, EyeOff, BrainCircuit, Users, Building2 } from 'lucide-react';
    12 import { UserType } from '@/types/types';
    13 
    14 const Login: React.FC = () => {
    15   const navigate = useNavigate();
    16   const { login, register, isAuthenticated, user } = useAuth();
    17 
    18   // 登录状态
    19   const [loginUsername, setLoginUsername] = useState('');
    20   const [loginPassword, setLoginPassword] = useState('');
    21   const [loginLoading, setLoginLoading] = useState(false);
    22   const [showLoginPwd, setShowLoginPwd] = useState(false);
    23 
    24   // 注册状态
    25   const [regUsername, setRegUsername] = useState('');
    26   const [regPassword, setRegPassword] = useState('');
    27   const [regDisplayName, setRegDisplayName] = useState('');
    28   const [regUserType, setRegUserType] = useState<UserType>('jobseeker');
    29   const [regCompanyName, setRegCompanyName] = useState('');
    30   const [regLoading, setRegLoading] = useState(false);
    31   const [showRegPwd, setShowRegPwd] = useState(false);
    32   const [agreed, setAgreed] = useState(false);
    33 
    34   // 如果已认证，跳转
    35   if (isAuthenticated && user) {
    36     if (user.role === 'admin' || user.user_type === 'admin') {
    37       navigate('/admin/users', { replace: true });
    38     } else if (user.user_type === 'enterprise') {
    39       navigate('/enterprise/home', { replace: true });
    40     } else {
    41       navigate('/jobseeker/home', { replace: true });
    42     }
    43     return null;
    44   }
    45 
    46   const handleLogin = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    47     e.preventDefault();
    48     if (!loginUsername || !loginPassword) return;
    49     setLoginLoading(true);
    50     try {
    51       await login(loginUsername, loginPassword);
    52     } finally {
    53       setLoginLoading(false);
    54     }
    55   };
    56 
    57   const handleRegister = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    58     e.preventDefault();
    59     if (!agreed) return;
    60     if (!regUsername || !regPassword || !regDisplayName) return;
    61     if (regUserType === 'enterprise' && !regCompanyName) return;
    62     setRegLoading(true);
    63     try {
    64       await register({
    65         username: regUsername,
    66         password: regPassword,
    67         display_name: regDisplayName,
    68         user_type: regUserType,
    69         company_name: regCompanyName,
    70       });
    71       // 注册成功后自动登录
    72       await login(regUsername, regPassword);
    73     } finally {
    74       setRegLoading(false);
    75     }
    76   };
    77 
    78   return (
    79     <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-12">
    80       <div className="w-full max-w-md">
    81         {/* Logo区域 */}
    82         <div className="text-center mb-8">
    83           <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl mb-4 border-solid border-[#94b2e4] bg-[#9bc6eb] bg-none border-[0px] border-[#a4c4e7]">
    84             <BrainCircuit className="w-8 h-8 text-primary-foreground" />
    85           </div>
    86           <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground text-balance">智聘未来</h1>
    87           <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1 text-pretty">Agent驱动的岗位智能匹配与能力图谱系统</p>
    88         </div>
    89 
    90         <Card className="shadow-lg border-border">
    91           <CardHeader className="pb-4">
    92             <CardTitle className="text-lg text-balance">欢迎使用</CardTitle>
    93             <CardDescription className="text-pretty">登录或注册以使用智能招聘服务</CardDescription>
    94           </CardHeader>
    95           <CardContent>
    96             <Tabs defaultValue="login">
    97               <TabsList className="grid grid-cols-2 w-full mb-6">
    98                 <TabsTrigger value="login">登录</TabsTrigger>
    99                 <TabsTrigger value="register">注册</TabsTrigger>
   100               </TabsList>
   101 
   102               {/* 登录Tab */}
   103               <TabsContent value="login">
   104                 <form onSubmit={handleLogin} className="space-y-4">
   105                   <div className="space-y-2">
   106                     <Label htmlFor="login-username" className="text-sm font-normal">用户名</Label>
   107                     <Input
   108                       id="login-username"
   109                       placeholder="请输入用户名"
   110                       value={loginUsername}
   111                       onChange={e => setLoginUsername(e.target.value.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, ''))}
   112                       required
   113                       autoComplete="username"
   114                       className="px-3"
   115                     />
   116                   </div>
   117                   <div className="space-y-2">
   118                     <Label htmlFor="login-password" className="text-sm font-normal">密码</Label>
   119                     <div className="relative">
   120                       <Input
   121                         id="login-password"
   122                         type={showLoginPwd ? 'text' : 'password'}
   123                         placeholder="请输入密码"
   124                         value={loginPassword}
   125                         onChange={e => setLoginPassword(e.target.value)}
   126                         required
   127                         autoComplete="current-password"
   128                         className="px-3 pr-10"
   129                       />
   130                       <button
   131                         type="button"
   132                         className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
   133                         onClick={() => setShowLoginPwd(v => !v)}
   134                         tabIndex={-1}
   135                       >
   136                         {showLoginPwd ? <EyeOff className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />}
   137                       </button>
   138                     </div>
   139                   </div>
   140                   <Button type="submit" className="w-full h-9 border-solid border-[#94b2e4] bg-[#9bc6eb] bg-none border-[0px] border-[#a4c4e7]" disabled={loginLoading}>
   141                     {loginLoading ? '登录中...' : '登录'}
   142                   </Button>
   143                 </form>
   144               </TabsContent>
   145 
   146               {/* 注册Tab */}
   147               <TabsContent value="register">
   148                 <form onSubmit={handleRegister} className="space-y-4">

   150                     <Label className="text-sm font-normal">账号类型</Label>
   151                     <RadioGroup
   152                       value={regUserType}

     1 import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2 import { TreeNode } from '@/types/types';
     3 import { ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Circle } from 'lucide-react';
     4 
     5 interface CapabilityTreeChartProps {
     6   data: TreeNode;
     7   depth?: number;
     8 }
     9 
    10 interface TreeNodeItemProps {
    11   node: TreeNode;
    12   depth: number;
    13   expanded?: boolean;
    14 }
    15 
    16 function TreeNodeItem({ node, depth }: TreeNodeItemProps) {
    17   const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(depth < 2);
    18   const hasChildren = node.children && node.children.length > 0;
    19   const indent = depth * 20;
    20 
    21   const getNodeColor = () => {
    22     if (depth === 0) return 'text-primary font-semibold text-base';
    23     if (depth === 1) return 'text-foreground font-medium';
    24     return 'text-muted-foreground text-sm';
    25   };
    26 
    27   const getBarColor = () => {
    28     if (node.value === undefined) return null;
    29     if (node.value >= 80) return 'bg-primary';
    30     if (node.value >= 60) return 'bg-chart-2';
    31     if (node.value >= 40) return 'bg-chart-4';
    32     return 'bg-muted-foreground';
    33   };
    34 
    35   return (
    36     <div>
    37       <div
    38         className={`flex items-center gap-2 py-1.5 rounded-sm hover:bg-muted/50 cursor-pointer transition-colors ${hasChildren ? '' : 'cursor-default'}`}
    39         style={{ paddingLeft: `${indent + 8}px` }}
    40         onClick={() => hasChildren && setIsExpanded(v => !v)}
    41       >
    42         <span className="shrink-0 w-4 h-4 flex items-center justify-center">
    43           {hasChildren ? (
    44             isExpanded ? <ChevronDown className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" /> : <ChevronRight className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
    45           ) : (
    46             <Circle className="w-2 h-2 text-muted-foreground fill-muted-foreground" />
    47           )}
    48         </span>
    49         <span className={`flex-1 min-w-0 truncate ${getNodeColor()}`}>{node.name}</span>
    50         {node.value !== undefined && (
    51           <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
    52             <div className="w-20 h-1.5 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden">
    53               <div
    54                 className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${getBarColor()}`}
    55                 style={{ width: `${node.value}%` }}
    56               />
    57             </div>
    58             <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground w-7 text-right">{node.value}</span>
    59           </div>
    60         )}
    61       </div>
    62       {hasChildren && isExpanded && (
    63         <div>
    64           {node.children!.map((child, i) => (
    65             <TreeNodeItem key={i} node={child} depth={depth + 1} />
    66           ))}
    67         </div>
    68       )}
    69     </div>
    70   );
    71 }
    72 
    73 export function CapabilityTreeChart({ data, depth = 0 }: CapabilityTreeChartProps) {
    74   return (
    75     <div className="w-full">
    76       <TreeNodeItem node={data} depth={depth} />
    77     </div>
    78   );
    79 }

    40       .eq('enterprise_id', user!.id);
    41 
    42     const jobs = Array.isArray(jobsData) ? jobsData : [];

    44 
    45     let applications: { status: string; match_score?: number }[] = [];
    46     if (jobIds.length > 0) {
    47       const { data } = await supabase
    48         .from('applications')

    50         .in('job_id', jobIds);

    54     const totalApplications = applications.length;
    55     const avgScore = applications.length > 0
    56       ? Math.round(applications.filter(a => a.match_score).reduce((s, a) => s + (a.match_score || 0), 0) / applications.filter(a => a.match_score).length)
    57       : 0;
    58     const offers = applications.filter(a => a.status === 'offer').length;
    59     const convRate = totalApplications > 0 ? Math.round((offers / totalApplications) * 100) : 0;
    60 
    61     setStats({
    62       totalJobs: jobs.length,
    63       totalApplications,
    64       avgMatchScore: avgScore,
    65       conversionRate: convRate,
    66     });
    67 
    68     // 状态分布
    69     const statusMap: Record<string, string> = {
    70       pending: '待审核', reviewing: '审核中', interview: '面试中', offer: '已录用', rejected: '已淘汰'
    71     };
    72     const statusCounts: Record<string, number> = {};
    73     applications.forEach(a => {
    74       const label = statusMap[a.status] || a.status;
    75       statusCounts[label] = (statusCounts[label] || 0) + 1;
    76     });
    77     setStatusData(Object.entries(statusCounts).map(([name, value]) => ({ name, value })));
    78 
    79     // 模拟周数据
    80     const days = ['周一', '周二', '周三', '周四', '周五', '周六', '周日'];
    81     setWeeklyData(days.map(day => ({
    82       day,
    83       applications: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) + 1,
    84       views: Math.floor(Math.random() * 50) + 10,
    85     })));
    86 
    87     setLoading(false);

     2 import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
     3 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';

    18 const DEFAULT_RADAR = [

    36 export default function TalentPool() {
    37   const { user } = useAuth();
    38   const [applications, setApplications] = useState<Application[]>([]);
    39   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    40   const [searchText, setSearchText] = useState('');
    41   const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState('all');
    42   const [selectedApp, setSelectedApp] = useState<Application | null>(null);
    43 
    44   useEffect(() => {
    45     if (user) fetchApplications();
    46   }, [user]);
    47 
    48   const fetchApplications = async () => {
    49     // 先获取企业职位
    50     const { data: jobsData } = await supabase
    51       .from('jobs')
    52       .select('id')
    53       .eq('enterprise_id', user!.id);
    54 
    55     const jobIds = Array.isArray(jobsData) ? jobsData.map((j: { id: string }) => j.id) : [];
    56     if (jobIds.length === 0) { setLoading(false); return; }
    57 
    58     const { data } = await supabase
    59       .from('applications')
    60       .select('*, job:jobs(title), applicant:profiles(id, display_name, username, location, bio)')
    61       .in('job_id', jobIds)
    62       .order('applied_at', { ascending: false })
    63       .limit(50);
    64 
    65     setApplications(Array.isArray(data) ? data as Application[] : []);
    66     setLoading(false);
    67   };
    68 
    69   const handleUpdateCandidateStatus = async (appId: string, status: string) => {
    70     const { error } = await supabase.from('applications').update({ candidate_status: status }).eq('id', appId);
    71     if (error) toast.error('更新失败');
    72     else {
    73       toast.success('候选人状态已更新');
    74       fetchApplications();
    75     }
    76   };
    77 
    78   const filteredApps = applications.filter(app => {
    79     const applicant = app.applicant as unknown as { display_name?: string; username?: string } | undefined;
    80     const matchName = !searchText ||
    81       applicant?.display_name?.includes(searchText) ||
    82       applicant?.username?.includes(searchText);
    83     const matchStatus = statusFilter === 'all' || app.candidate_status === statusFilter;
    84     return matchName && matchStatus;
    85   });
    86 
    87   return (
    88     <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 md:px-8 py-6 space-y-6">
    89       <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground text-balance">人才库管理</h1>
    90 
    91       {/* 筛选区 */}
    92       <Card>
    93         <CardContent className="p-4">
    94           <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
    95             <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 relative">
    96               <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
    97               <Input
    98                 placeholder="搜索候选人姓名..."
    99                 value={searchText}
   100                 onChange={e => setSearchText(e.target.value)}
   101                 className="pl-9 px-3"
   102               />
   103             </div>
   104             <Select value={statusFilter} onValueChange={setStatusFilter}>
   105               <SelectTrigger className="w-36 shrink-0">
   106                 <SelectValue />
   107               </SelectTrigger>
   108               <SelectContent>
   109                 <SelectItem value="all">全部状态</SelectItem>
   110                 <SelectItem value="interested">感兴趣</SelectItem>
   111                 <SelectItem value="pending">待定</SelectItem>
   112                 <SelectItem value="unmatched">不匹配</SelectItem>
   113               </SelectContent>
   114             </Select>
   115           </div>
   116         </CardContent>
   117       </Card>
   118 
   119       {/* 候选人列表 */}
   120       <div className="space-y-1 mb-2">
   121         <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">共 {filteredApps.length} 位候选人</p>
   122       </div>
   123 
   124       {loading ? (
   125         <div className="space-y-3">{Array(4).fill(0).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-20 bg-muted" />)}</div>
   126       ) : filteredApps.length === 0 ? (
   127         <Card><CardContent className="py-16 text-center text-muted-foreground">
   128           <Users className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3" />
   129           暂无候选人，等待求职者投递
   130         </CardContent></Card>
   131       ) : (
   132         <div className="space-y-3">
   133           {filteredApps.map(app => {
   134             const applicant = app.applicant as unknown as { display_name?: string; username?: string; location?: string; bio?: string };
   135             const job = app.job as unknown as { title?: string };
   136             return (
   137               <Card key={app.id} className="hover:shadow-md transition-shadow">
   138                 <CardContent className="p-4">
   139                   <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3 flex-wrap">
   140                     <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 space-y-1">
   141                       <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
   142                         <span className="font-semibold text-foreground">
   143                           {applicant?.display_name || applicant?.username || '未知候选人'}
   144                         </span>
   145                         {app.match_score && (
   146                           <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs text-primary border-primary/30">
   147                             <TrendingUp className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />{app.match_score}% 匹配
   148                           </Badge>
   149                         )}
   150                         {app.candidate_status === 'interested' && <Badge className="text-xs bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/20">感兴趣</Badge>}
   151                         {app.candidate_status === 'unmatched' && <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-xs">不匹配</Badge>}
   152                       </div>
   153                       <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
   154                         申请岗位：{job?.title || '未知职位'} · {new Date(app.applied_at).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN')}
   155                       </p>
   156                       {applicant?.location && <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{applicant.location}</p>}
   157                     </div>
   158                     <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0 flex-wrap">
   159                       <Select
   160                         value={app.candidate_status || 'pending'}
   161                         onValueChange={v => handleUpdateCandidateStatus(app.id, v)}
   162                       >
   163                         <SelectTrigger className="w-24 h-8 text-xs">
   164                           <SelectValue />
   165                         </SelectTrigger>
   166                         <SelectContent>
   167                           <SelectItem value="interested">感兴趣</SelectItem>
   168                           <SelectItem value="pending">待定</SelectItem>
   169                           <SelectItem value="unmatched">不匹配</SelectItem>
   170                         </SelectContent>
   171                       </Select>
   172                       <Dialog>
   173                         <DialogTrigger asChild>
   174                           <Button
   175                             size="sm"
   176                             variant="outline"
   177                             className="h-8"
   178                             onClick={() => setSelectedApp(app)}
   179                           >
   180                             <Eye className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-1.5" />能力图谱
   181                           </Button>
   182                         </DialogTrigger>
   183                         <DialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
   184                           <DialogHeader>
   185                             <DialogTitle>
   186                               {applicant?.display_name || applicant?.username} 的能力图谱对比
   187                             </DialogTitle>
   188                           </DialogHeader>
   189                           <div className="pt-2">
   190                             <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-4">绿色为候选人能力，橙色为岗位要求</p>
   191                             <CapabilityRadarChart
   192                               data={DEFAULT_RADAR}
   193                               compareData={JOB_RADAR}
   194                               height={280}
   195                             />
   196                             <div className="mt-4 p-3 bg-primary/5 rounded-md border border-primary/20">
   197                               <p className="text-sm font-medium text-primary">综合匹配度：{app.match_score || 72}%</p>

   199                             </div>
   200                           </div>
   201                         </DialogContent>
   202                       </Dialog>
   203                     </div>
   204                   </div>
   205                 </CardContent>
   206               </Card>
   207             );
   208           })}
   209         </div>
   210       )}
   211     </div>
   212   );
   213 }

Path: [/workspace/app-bhs9a5otro5d/src/components/charts/CapabilityTreeImage.tsx]
Thought: 
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
import React, { useMemo } from 'react';
import { TreeNode } from '@/types/types';

// ─── 颜色配置（蓝色系）───────────────────────────────────────────
const NODE_COLORS = [
  { fill: '#1A4FA8', text: '#ffffff', stroke: '#1A4FA8' }, // 根节点：深蓝
  { fill: '#2563EB', text: '#ffffff', stroke: '#2563EB' }, // 一级：亮蓝
  { fill: '#3B82F6', text: '#ffffff', stroke: '#3B82F6' }, // 二级：中蓝
  { fill: '#DBEAFE', text: '#1e3a8a', stroke: '#93C5FD' }, // 三级：浅蓝
];

const EDGE_COLOR = '#BFDBFE';
const BAR_BG = '#E0EFFE';
const BAR_FG_HIGH = '#1A4FA8';
const BAR_FG_MID = '#3B82F6';
const BAR_FG_LOW = '#93C5FD';
const VALUE_COLOR = '#1e3a8a';

// ─── 布局常量 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const NODE_W = 90;     // 节点宽
const NODE_H = 32;     // 节点高
const RADIUS = 8;      // 圆角
const H_GAP = 20;      // 同层节点水平间距
const V_GAP = 60;      // 层间垂直间距
const LEAF_BAR_H = 8;  // 叶子节点值条高度
const PADDING = 16;    // 整体边距

// ─── 布局计算 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
interface LayoutNode {
  node: TreeNode;
  x: number;       // 中心 x
  y: number;       // 顶部 y
  depth: number;
  width: number;   // 子树宽度
  children: LayoutNode[];
}

function calcLeafWidth(node: TreeNode): number {
  if (!node.children || node.children.length === 0) return NODE_W;
  return node.children.reduce((sum, c) => sum + calcLeafWidth(c) + H_GAP, -H_GAP);
}

function buildLayout(node: TreeNode, depth: number, offsetX: number): LayoutNode {
  const subtreeW = calcLeafWidth(node);
  const cx = offsetX + subtreeW / 2;
  const y = PADDING + depth * (NODE_H + V_GAP);

  if (!node.children || node.children.length === 0) {
    return { node, x: cx, y, depth, width: subtreeW, children: [] };
  }

  let childX = offsetX;
  const children: LayoutNode[] = node.children.map(child => {
    const cw = calcLeafWidth(child);
    const laid = buildLayout(child, depth + 1, childX);
    childX += cw + H_GAP;
    return laid;
  });

  return { node, x: cx, y, depth, width: subtreeW, children };
}

function collectNodes(layout: LayoutNode, acc: LayoutNode[] = []): LayoutNode[] {
  acc.push(layout);
  layout.children.forEach(c => collectNodes(c, acc));
  return acc;
}

function collectEdges(layout: LayoutNode, acc: { from: LayoutNode; to: LayoutNode }[] = []) {
  layout.children.forEach(c => {
    acc.push({ from: layout, to: c });
    collectEdges(c, acc);
  });
  return acc;
}

// ─── 单节点渲染 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function NodeRect({ layout }: { layout: LayoutNode }) {
  const { node, x, y, depth } = layout;
  const color = NODE_COLORS[Math.min(depth, NODE_COLORS.length - 1)];
  const nx = x - NODE_W / 2;
  const isLeaf = !node.children || node.children.length === 0;
  const hasValue = isLeaf && node.value !== undefined;

  const barFill =
    node.value !== undefined
      ? node.value >= 75 ? BAR_FG_HIGH
        : node.value >= 50 ? BAR_FG_MID
        : BAR_FG_LOW
      : BAR_FG_LOW;

  const barWidth = hasValue ? Math.round((node.value! / 100) * (NODE_W - 16)) : 0;

  return (
    <g>
      {/* 节点背景 */}
      <rect
        x={nx}
        y={y}
        width={NODE_W}
        height={NODE_H}
        rx={RADIUS}
        ry={RADIUS}
        fill={color.fill}
        stroke={color.stroke}
        strokeWidth={1.5}
      />
      {/* 节点标签 */}
      <text
        x={x}
        y={y + (hasValue ? 12 : NODE_H / 2 + 4.5)}
        textAnchor="middle"
        fontSize={depth === 0 ? 12 : 11}
        fontWeight={depth <= 1 ? 600 : 400}
        fill={color.text}
        fontFamily="Inter, system-ui, sans-serif"
      >
        {node.name.length > 7 ? node.name.slice(0, 6) + '…' : node.name}
      </text>
      {/* 能力值条 */}
      {hasValue && (
        <>
          <rect
            x={nx + 8}
            y={y + NODE_H - LEAF_BAR_H - 4}
            width={NODE_W - 16}
            height={LEAF_BAR_H}
            rx={3}
            fill={BAR_BG}
          />
          <rect
            x={nx + 8}
            y={y + NODE_H - LEAF_BAR_H - 4}
            width={barWidth}
            height={LEAF_BAR_H}
            rx={3}
            fill={barFill}
          />
          <text
            x={nx + NODE_W + 3}
            y={y + NODE_H - 4}
            fontSize={9}
            fill={VALUE_COLOR}
            fontFamily="Inter, system-ui, sans-serif"
          >
            {node.value}
          </text>
        </>
      )}
    </g>
  );
}

// ─── 连线（贝塞尔曲线）────────────────────────────────────────────
function Edge({ from, to }: { from: LayoutNode; to: LayoutNode }) {
  const x1 = from.x;
  const y1 = from.y + NODE_H;
  const x2 = to.x;
  const y2 = to.y;
  const cy1 = y1 + (y2 - y1) * 0.5;
  const cy2 = y1 + (y2 - y1) * 0.5;
  return (
    <path
      d={`M ${x1} ${y1} C ${x1} ${cy1}, ${x2} ${cy2}, ${x2} ${y2}`}
      fill="none"
      stroke={EDGE_COLOR}
      strokeWidth={1.5}
      strokeLinecap="round"
    />
  );
}

// ─── 主组件 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
interface CapabilityTreeImageProps {
  data: TreeNode;
  className?: string;
}

export function CapabilityTreeImage({ data, className = '' }: CapabilityTreeImageProps) {
  const { layout, svgWidth, svgHeight } = useMemo(() => {
    const layout = buildLayout(data, 0, PADDING);
    const allNodes = collectNodes(layout);
    // 计算画布尺寸
    const maxX = Math.max(...allNodes.map(n => n.x + NODE_W / 2 + PADDING));
    const maxY = Math.max(...allNodes.map(n => n.y + NODE_H + PADDING + (n.node.value !== undefined ? 14 : 0)));
    return {
      layout,
      svgWidth: Math.max(maxX + PADDING, 280),
      svgHeight: Math.max(maxY + PADDING, 120),
    };
  }, [data]);

  const allNodes = collectNodes(layout);
  const allEdges = collectEdges(layout);

  return (
    <div className={`w-full overflow-x-auto ${className}`}>
      <svg
        viewBox={`0 0 ${svgWidth} ${svgHeight}`}
        width="100%"
        style={{ minWidth: Math.min(svgWidth, 280), maxWidth: svgWidth, display: 'block' }}
        aria-label="能力树图"
        role="img"
      >
        {/* 背景 */}
        <rect width={svgWidth} height={svgHeight} fill="#F0F7FF" rx={12} />
        {/* 连线（先渲染，在节点下层） */}
        <g>
          {allEdges.map((e, i) => (
            <Edge key={i} from={e.from} to={e.to} />
          ))}
        </g>
        {/* 节点 */}
        <g>
          {allNodes.map((n, i) => (
            <NodeRect key={i} layout={n} />
          ))}
        </g>
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}

```

import { Search, Users, TrendingUp, Eye } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

const DEFAULT_RADAR = [
  { subject: '编程技能', value: 75 },
  { subject: '系统设计', value: 60 },

     1 import React from 'react';
     2 import {
     3   RadarChart, PolarGrid, PolarAngleAxis, PolarRadiusAxis,
     4   Radar, ResponsiveContainer, Tooltip, Legend
     5 } from 'recharts';
     6 
     7 interface RadarDataItem {
     8   subject: string;
     9   value: number;
    10   fullMark?: number;
    11 }
    12 
    13 interface CapabilityRadarChartProps {
    14   data: RadarDataItem[];
    15   color?: string;
    16   compareData?: RadarDataItem[];
    17   compareColor?: string;
    18   height?: number;
    19 }
    20 
    21 const CustomTooltip = ({ active, payload }: { active?: boolean; payload?: Array<{ value: number; name: string }> }) => {
    22   if (active && payload && payload.length) {
    23     return (
    24       <div className="bg-card border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 shadow-sm text-sm">
    25         {payload.map((p, i) => (
    26           <div key={i} className="flex items-center gap-2">
    27             <span className="text-muted-foreground">{p.name}:</span>
    28             <span className="font-medium">{p.value}</span>
    29           </div>
    30         ))}
    31       </div>
    32     );
    33   }
    34   return null;
    35 };
    36 
    37 export function CapabilityRadarChart({
    38   data,
    39   color = 'hsl(161, 48%, 20%)',
    40   compareData,
    41   compareColor = 'hsl(22, 89%, 54%)',
    42   height = 300,
    43 }: CapabilityRadarChartProps) {
    44   const mergedData = data.map((item, i) => ({
    45     subject: item.subject,
    46     个人能力: item.value,
    47     ...(compareData && compareData[i] ? { 岗位要求: compareData[i].value } : {}),
    48     fullMark: item.fullMark || 100,
    49   }));
    50 
    51   return (
    52     <div className="w-full min-w-0 overflow-hidden">
    53       <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={height}>
    54         <RadarChart data={mergedData} margin={{ top: 10, right: 30, bottom: 10, left: 30 }}>
    55           <PolarGrid stroke="hsl(var(--border))" />
    56           <PolarAngleAxis
    57             dataKey="subject"
    58             tick={{ fontSize: 12, fill: 'hsl(var(--muted-foreground))' }}
    59           />
    60           <PolarRadiusAxis
    61             angle={30}
    62             domain={[0, 100]}
    63             tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: 'hsl(var(--muted-foreground))' }}
    64           />
    65           <Radar
    66             name="个人能力"
    67             dataKey="个人能力"
    68             stroke={color}
    69             fill={color}
    70             fillOpacity={0.2}
    71           />
    72           {compareData && (
    73             <Radar
    74               name="岗位要求"
    75               dataKey="岗位要求"
    76               stroke={compareColor}
    77               fill={compareColor}
    78               fillOpacity={0.15}
    79             />
    80           )}
    81           <Tooltip content={<CustomTooltip />} />
    82           {compareData && <Legend wrapperStyle={{ paddingTop: 8 }} layout="horizontal" />}
    83         </RadarChart>
    84       </ResponsiveContainer>
    85     </div>
    86   );
    87 }

     1 import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
     2 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     3 import { AuthContextType, Profile, RegisterData } from '@/types/types';
     4 import { toast } from 'sonner';
     5 
     6 const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
     7 
     8 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
     9   const [user, setUser] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    10   const [session, setSession] = useState<unknown>(null);
    11   const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
    12 
    13   const fetchProfile = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {
    14     const { data, error } = await supabase
    15       .from('profiles')
    16       .select('*')
    17       .eq('id', userId)
    18       .maybeSingle();
    19     if (error) {
    20       console.error('获取用户信息失败:', error);
    21       return null;
    22     }
    23     return data as Profile | null;
    24   }, []);
    25 
    26   const refreshProfile = useCallback(async () => {
    27     const { data: { session: currentSession } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
    28     if (currentSession?.user) {
    29       const profile = await fetchProfile(currentSession.user.id);
    30       setUser(profile);
    31     }
    32   }, [fetchProfile]);
    33 
    34   useEffect(() => {
    35     // 初始化获取session
    36     supabase.auth.getSession().then(async ({ data: { session: s } }) => {
    37       setSession(s);
    38       if (s?.user) {
    39         const profile = await fetchProfile(s.user.id);
    40         setUser(profile);
    41       }
    42       setIsLoading(false);
    43     });
    44 
    45     // 监听auth状态变化
    46     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (event, s) => {
    47       setSession(s);
    48       if (s?.user) {
    49         const profile = await fetchProfile(s.user.id);
    50         setUser(profile);
    51       } else {
    52         setUser(null);
    53       }
    54       if (event === 'SIGNED_IN') {
    55         setIsLoading(false);
    56       }
    57     });
    58 
    59     return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
    60   }, [fetchProfile]);
    61 
    62   const login = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    63     const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
    64     const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
    65     if (error) {
    66       toast.error('登录失败：' + (error.message.includes('Invalid') ? '用户名或密码错误' : error.message));
    67       throw error;
    68     }
    69     toast.success('登录成功');
    70   };
    71 
    72   const register = async (data: RegisterData) => {
    73     const email = `${data.username}@miaoda.com`;
    74     const { data: authData, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
    75       email,
    76       password: data.password,
    77       options: {
    78         data: {
    79           username: data.username,
    80           display_name: data.display_name,
    81           user_type: data.user_type,
    82         }
    83       }
    84     });
    85     if (error) {
    86       if (error.message.includes('already registered') || error.message.includes('unique')) {
    87         toast.error('注册失败：用户名已存在');
    88       } else {
    89         toast.error('注册失败：' + error.message);
    90       }
    91       throw error;
    92     }
    93 
    94     // 如果是企业用户，创建企业信息
    95     if (data.user_type === 'enterprise' && data.company_name && authData.user) {
    96       await supabase.from('enterprise_profiles').insert({
    97         profile_id: authData.user.id,
    98         company_name: data.company_name,
    99       });
   100     }
   101 
   102     toast.success('注册成功，欢迎加入！');
   103   };
   104 
   105   const logout = async () => {
   106     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   107     setUser(null);
   108     setSession(null);
   109     toast.success('已退出登录');
   110   };
   111 
   112   const value: AuthContextType = {
   113     user,
   114     session,
   115     isLoading,
   116     isAuthenticated: !!user,
   117     login,
   118     register,
   119     logout,
   120     refreshProfile,
   121   };
   122 
   123   return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;
   124 }
   125 
   126 export function useAuth() {
   127   const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   128   if (!context) {
   129     throw new Error('useAuth 必须在 AuthProvider 内部使用');
   130   }
   131   return context;
   132 }
   133

     2 import React from 'react';
     3 import { Toaster as Sonner } from "@/components/ui/sonner";
     4 import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
     5 import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from "@tanstack/react-query";
     6 import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route } from "react-router-dom";
     7 import { AuthProvider } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";
     8 import { AppLayout } from "@/components/layouts/AppLayout";
     9 import { routes } from "@/routes";
    10 
    11 const queryClient = new QueryClient({
    12   defaultOptions: {
    13     queries: { retry: 1, refetchOnWindowFocus: false },
    14   },
    15 });
    16 
    17 const App = () => (
    18   <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
    19     <AuthProvider>
    20       <TooltipProvider>
    21         <Sonner />
    22         <BrowserRouter>
    23           <Routes>
    24             {routes.map(({ path, element }) => {
    25               // 登录页不需要Layout
    26               const isAuthPage = path === '/login';
    27               return (
    28                 <Route
    29                   key={path}
    30                   path={path}
    31                   element={isAuthPage ? element : <AppLayout>{element}</AppLayout>}
    32                 />
    33               );
    34             })}
    35           </Routes>
    36         </BrowserRouter>
    37       </TooltipProvider>
    38     </AuthProvider>
    39   </QueryClientProvider>

];

function getNavItems(userType: string | undefined, role: string | undefined) {
  if (role === 'admin' || userType === 'admin') return adminNavItems;
  if (userType === 'enterprise') return enterpriseNavItems;
  return jobseekerNavItems;
}

function getHomeRoute(userType: string | undefined, role: string | undefined) {
  if (role === 'admin' || userType === 'admin') return '/admin/users';
  if (userType === 'enterprise') return '/enterprise/home';
  return '/jobseeker/home';
}

  variant?: 'sidebar' | 'top';
}

  const { user, logout, isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  const location = useLocation();

AgentThinkAction(thought='Found the root cause! \n\nThe `has_role` function queries the `profiles` table itself:\n```sql\nSELECT EXISTS (\n  SELECT 1 FROM profiles p WHERE p.id = uid AND p.role = role_name::user_role\n);\n```\n\nAnd there\'s a policy "管理员可完全访问profiles" that uses `has_role()` - this creates a **circular RLS dependency**:\n\n1. User queries `profiles` table\n2. RLS policy "管理员可完全访问profiles" calls `has_role()`\n3. `has_role()` queries `profiles` table again\n4. Which triggers RLS again → infinite recursion!\n\nThis infinite recursion causes the `fetchProfile` query to hang indefinitely, which is why the login button stays "登录中..." forever.\n\nThe fix: The `has_role` function needs to use `SECURITY DEFINER` or bypass RLS, OR the admin policy should use a different approach (like `auth.uid()` directly checking a JWT claim, or using `SET search_path` tricks).\n\nThe simplest fix: make the `has_role` function `SECURITY DEFINER` so it bypasses RLS when querying profiles. Or alternatively, rewrite the admin policy to not use `has_role` but instead directly check using a subquery that bypasses RLS.\n\nActually, using `SECURITY DEFINER` on the helper function is the correct approach per the guidelines. Let me fix the `has_role` function to be `SECURITY DEFINER`.\n\nAlso there\'s another issue: the policy "所有认证用户可查看公开profile" has `qual: true` - this means all authenticated users can SELECT from profiles. This policy alone should allow fetchProfile to work without hitting the recursive policy. But maybe the admin ALL policy is evaluated first and causes the recursion.\n\nActually, RLS policies are evaluated with OR - if ANY policy allows access, the row is accessible. The "所有认证用户可查看公开profile" SELECT policy with `qual: true` should be sufficient for SELECT. But maybe the "管理员可完全访问profiles" ALL policy with its recursive call is causing a stack overflow/deadlock that prevents any query from completing.\n\nThe fix: \n1. Make `has_role` SECURITY DEFINER so it bypasses RLS\n2. This breaks the infinite recursion\n\nLet me also check: does the `uid()` function exist? <action>
**MCPAction**
THOUGHT: 找到根本原因了！**RLS 策略循环递归**：

- `profiles` 表有一条管理员策略调用了 `has_role()` 函数
- `has_role()` 函数内部又查询了 `profiles` 表
- 这导致无限递归 → 查询永久挂起 → 按钮卡在"登录中..."

修复方式：给 `has_role` 函数加上 `SECURITY DEFINER`，绕过 RLS 递归：
NAME: supabase_apply_migration

**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.AGENT)
CONTENT: `prosecdef: true` 确认已生效。

---

**问题根因**：`profiles` 表的管理员 RLS 策略调用 `has_role()` 函数，该函数又反过来查询 `profiles` 表，触发 RLS，形成**无限递归**。数据库查询永远不返回，导致登录后 `fetchProfile` 永久挂起，按钮卡在"登录中..."。

**修复方案**：为 `has_role()` 函数添加 `SECURITY DEFINER` + `SET search_path = public`，让函数以定义者权限执行，绕过 RLS 检查，打破递归循环。现在刷新页面重新登录即可正常进入系统。
</action>

AgentThinkAction(thought='Now I see the critical bug clearly!\n\nIn Login.tsx, lines 35-44:\n```tsx\n// 如果已认证，跳转\nif (isAuthenticated && user) {\n  if (user.role === \'admin\' || user.user_type === \'admin\') {\n    navigate(\'/admin/users\', { replace: true });\n  } else if (user.user_type === \'enterprise\') {\n    navigate(\'/enterprise/home\', { replace: true });\n  } else {\n    navigate(\'/jobseeker/home\', { replace: true });\n  }\n  return null;\n}\n```\n\n**This is called directly in the component body (render function), NOT inside a useEffect!**\n\nCalling `navigate()` during render is a React anti-pattern and causes issues. In React 18 with strict mode and concurrent rendering, calling side effects during render causes problems.\n\nBut more critically: **`navigate` is called on EVERY RENDER when `isAuthenticated && user` is true**. This is problematic but should work for redirecting.\n\nThe REAL issue is different. Let me look at the flow:\n\n1. User is not logged in → Login renders → `isAuthenticated` is false → form shows\n2. User clicks 登录 → `handleLogin` called → `setLoginLoading(true)` → component re-renders\n3. Re-render: `isAuthenticated` still false → form shows with "登录中..."\n4. `login()` called → `signInWithPassword` → 200 OK → login() resolves\n5. `finally: setLoginLoading(false)` → `setLoginLoading` triggers re-render\n6. BEFORE this re-render: `onAuthStateChange` fires → `setUser(profile)` → another re-render queued\n\nBut wait - React batches state updates. The `setLoginLoading(false)` and `setUser(profile)` might not fire in the right order.\n\nActually, there\'s a subtle issue. The `handleLogin` function:\n```tsx\nconst handleLogin = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {\n  e.preventDefault();\n  if (!loginUsername || !loginPassword) return;\n  setLoginLoading(true);\n  try {\n    await login(loginUsername, loginPassword);\n  } finally {\n    setLoginLoading(false);\n  }\n};\n```\n\nWhen `login()` resolves successfully (no error), the finally block runs `setLoginLoading(false)`. This is a state update inside an async callback. In React 18, this IS batched with other pending state updates.\n\nBut actually the issue is this: `login()` resolves as soon as `signInWithPassword` returns. ```
New String: ```
const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);

/** 从 auth.User 元数据中构建兜底 profile，避免 fetchProfile 失败时用户卡在登录页 */
function buildFallbackProfile(authUser: User): Profile {
  const meta = authUser.user_metadata ?? {};
  const email = authUser.email ?? '';
  const username = meta.username ?? email.split('@')[0] ?? authUser.id;
  return {
    id: authUser.id,
    username,
    email,
    display_name: meta.display_name ?? username,
    user_type: meta.user_type ?? 'jobseeker',
    role: meta.role ?? 'user',
    avatar_url: meta.avatar_url ?? null,
    bio: null,
    location: null,
    website: null,
    phone: null,
    created_at: authUser.created_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    updated_at: authUser.updated_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
  } as Profile;
}
```

Makes the HTTP POST to auth/v1/token → 200 OK\n2. Internally processes the response (stores session, etc.)\n3. Triggers `onAuthStateChange` with SIGNED_IN\n4.
